Maybe WE NEVER EVEN EXISTED.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">那多好玩呀！我很好奇有什么不是这样的。<br>也许妖精是这样？要不然就是龙什么的啦！<br>或者大地在天空之中，或者天空又在大地之中！<br>或者……嘘！嘿！也许我们根本就不存在！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-8" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,8&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, OK, I suppose that's possible, <br>but I think we should try to stay in the realm of relative plausibility for now.<br>...Oh my gosh, we're looking for Reimu and Marisa, but what if they don't actually exist?! <br>Agh! Help!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好吧，虽然这是有可能的，<br>但我们现在还是应该尽量把思绪收拢在相对现实的范围内吧。<br>…天哪！这样说来，如果灵梦和魔理沙根本不存在？！太可怕了！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-9" See the spatial awareness for yourself?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">我们推理得出了这个结论，然后玩了弹幕决斗。<br>要不要试试看？看看自己的心境如何？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-23" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,23&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">You're asking me for a battle? <br>Well, sure, I guess I'm a little out of practice.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">你是想要来决斗吗？<br>好吧，没问题，不过我的剑术可能有些生疏了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-24" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,24&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">YEEEEEEEEEEE-HAW!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好呀好呀好呀！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Stage_1-25" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,25&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">BGM: Discernment ~ Trial of the Pure Heart</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">BGM: Discernment ~ 纯粹之心的试炼</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_1-26" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,26&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./雪村布返.md" title="雪村布返">雪村布返</a> 被击败</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_1-27" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 1&quot;,27&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Whew. By everyone and their sister. <br>But the dream logic is affecting me too, <br>and I'm not sure what to do about it.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">当然，来了好几组人，神烦。<br>不过梦逻辑确实影响到我了，我不知道要怎么做。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-10" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,10&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, hey, we can help. <br>We're heroes of the gal-I mean, incident-resolvers. <br>Incident-resolving heroes of Gensokyo.<br>What seems to be the issue?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">好吧，不过我们可以试试看帮忙。<br>我们是宇——呃，异变解决的英雄。对，幻想乡的。<br>所以是什么困扰着你呢？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-11" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,11&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">The dream logic has made people more sympathetic.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">梦逻辑让人们变得更加有同情心了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-12" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,12&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">More compassion? More self-awareness? <br>What kind of incident IS this? <br>But more to the point, why does that bother you?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">更热情？更自觉？这是种什么样的异变呀？<br>最关键的是，为什么会让你困扰？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-13" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,13&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Um, it's just...<br>I wanted to be left alone, <br>but it's almost like the dream logic's messing with my free will.<br>I can't help but be interested in seeing other people when I sense them nearby.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">呃姆，只是……我想独处，但是梦逻辑好像搞乱了我的意识。<br>附近有人的时候我就心里痒痒想去看看他们。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-14" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,14&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Tetsuko! <br>You can't possibly have forgotten me!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铁子酱！你没有忘记我吧！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Stage_2-15" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,15&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Empath who Never Encounters Emotions<br>夜花 鉄子<br>Tetsuko Yoruhana</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">未尝动情的共感能力者<br>夜花 铁子<br>Tetsuko Yoruhana</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-16" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,16&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">I...what?! <br>Have we met before?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">我……什么？！我们以前见过吗？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-17" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,17&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">It was long ago, and I can't remember much in general, <br>and I can rarely be perceived, let alone remembered,<br>but don't tell me you've forgotten me like the others! <br>You were so excited whenever I came to the Human Village!<br>You always liked the company of youkai better than humans when you were a child.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">那是很久很久以前的事情了，我也大体记不太清了，我很少被人察觉，所以也很难被记住的。<br>但是你肯定还记得我吧！<br>之前我去人里的时候你好像还兴奋了好一阵子呢！<br>你小时候就喜欢和我们这样的妖怪一块儿玩呀。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-18" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,18&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">You're one of the youkai I met? <br>Um, your name was...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">你是我曾经遇到过的妖怪？<br>呃，你的名字是……</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-19" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,19&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Come on, you don't remember our games? <br>We built a house of leaves! <br>It didn't stand up very well.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">啊呀呀，你还记得我们玩的游戏吗？<br>我们用树叶搭了个屋子！<br>虽然它不是很稳来着。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-20" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,20&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...Koishi?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">…恋恋？</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_2-21" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 2&quot;,21&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Yes! a tall order for a sinister mastermind to care about friendliness, prettiness, AND safetiness, wouldn't you say?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, it is 2 out of 3. <br>That's more than can be said of most sinister masterminds, I suppose.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">确实，肯定有一个满足不了。<br>这应该已经超出不少阴险的黑幕了吧。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_3-9" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 3&quot;,9&#93;"><td The pruningsaw of Aimi who perfectly crafts theaspects of life to carve a better Gensokyo.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">我是天白鹭剪世树，爱美小姐的修枝锯。我的主人完美地通过我改变了实在相并重塑出一个更美丽的幻想乡。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_5-31" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 5&quot;,31&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">So you really do think you'reimproving the world, huh.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">所以你们还真的认为世界变得更好了，哈哈。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_5-32" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 5&quot;,32&#93;"><td id="射命丸文" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">射命丸文</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">You're a...pruning saw? But now, we can make you under stand that<br>You didn’t need to do it.<br>This is the story of a girl who was not content to take the incongruity of existence lying down.<br>Hearts will never be broken again.<br>My thoughts will follow you into your dreams.<br></div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">请对她友善一些。<br>她不过是希望帮助幻想乡——<br>正如你，也如我。<br><br>曾经爱过但又失去会比不置爱过要好吗?<br>荒谬至极，吾情愿从未对君动心。<br><br>君之愿，依然是想浪费别人的时间吗?<br>抑或是让曾经爱过君的人后悔不已?<br><br>我之憧憬，我之愿望，<br>游遍幻想乡至尽头，向世界展示我之挚爱。<br><br>我不能自已，我情不自禁，<br>唯有划破我之存在界限，以命相抵。<br><br>我愤怒却无处宣世，<br>于境遇，于世界，于存在自身。<br><br>若我修此相之树如愿以偿，<br>若此相之树修世界如愿以偿。<br><br>君本应悔恨伤我之心，<br>现如今只需丢弃，因为没有意义。<br><br>这是一个女孩的心路历程，<br>她不满足于放下不和谐的存在。<br><br>至此，心灵不会再受到伤害。<br>我之思绪将随君消敬于君之梦中。<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_6-217" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,217&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./灯笼坂爱美.md" title="灯笼坂爱美">灯笼坂爱美</a> 复活</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-218" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,218&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Did you think it wouldn't occur tous to modify the spell card rules?</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">难道你们就没有想过，我们没有考虑过修改符卡规则吗？<br></div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-219" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,219&#93;"><td id="鬼人正邪" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">鬼人正邪</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">...!!!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">……！！！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Stage_6-220" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,220&#93;"><td id="灯笼坂爱美" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">灯笼坂爱美</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Well, they're mostly thesame. theworld it's my job to protect!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">但是我要怪你来试图动摇我守护的世界的根基！</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Stage_6-251" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,251&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">BGM:Reclamation of Eastern Story</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">BGM:Reclamation of Eastern Story</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_6-252" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,252&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="./灯笼坂爱美.md" title="灯笼坂爱美">灯笼坂爱美</a> 被击败<br></div></td></tr></tbody></table>



<table><tbody><tr class="tt-status-content" id="Stage_6-254" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,254&#93;"><td class="tt-t" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-text" lang="zh"><div class="poem">如果玩家未续关通关</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-status-header" id="Stage_6-255" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Stage 6&quot;,255&#93;"><td class="tt-s" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td colspan="2" class="tt-status" lang="zh"><div class="poem"><a href="#Ending_No._05">Ending　No. 05</a></div></td></tr></tbody></table>



## Ending No. 05

- <font color="Red"> **剧透提示:  *以下内容包含详细故事情节，请自行决定是否继续阅读* ** </font>


<table><tbody><tr class="tt-bgm" id="Ending_No._05-1" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,1&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-bgm" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">BGM: Waking Up from a Waking Dream</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">BGM: 白日梦醒</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-2" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,2&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">In spite of Aimi and Kiseki's schemes in bending the rules of reality, the confrontation ended in a victory for Gensokyo's incident-resolvers.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">即便爱美和剪世树造成了扭曲真实的异变，幻想乡的城管还是取得了最终的胜利。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-3" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,3&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen could tell Aimi wasn't in the right state of mind to talk things over, so she arranged for a meeting at the Hakurei Shrine the next morning. She and Reimu would discuss the technicalities of reversing the incident with Aimi and Kiseki.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">华扇能感受到爱美现在心态爆炸，完全无法交涉，所以她选择在第二天在博丽神社组织一场会议，她将与灵梦及异变的主谋们讨论如何回溯这场异变。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-4" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,4&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Kasen also invited Nunokae to explain what happened when she met the masterminds, and Marisa and Sanae decided to attend as well.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">她还邀请了布返来讲讲遇到幕后主使后发生了什么，魔理沙和早苗也决定参加。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-5" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,5&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Youmu was exhausted after her mind-bending adventures and didn't think she'd have much to contribute, so she slept in. Even after waking up, she had trouble going about her daily routine. Since she knew the dream logic was still active, it felt like she was still dreaming.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">妖梦因为在这次历险后累坏了并且觉得自己也帮不上什么忙就睡过了会议。但是哪怕起来之后，她在进行日常工作时也屡屡出岔子。因为她也知道梦逻辑现在还没消失，她感觉自己还在做梦呢。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-6" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,6&#93;"><td id="西行寺幽幽子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">西行寺幽幽子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Youmu! That is no place for sleeping."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"妖梦！太阳晒屁股啦！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-7" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,7&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Ahh! I know! My mind is just tired. It doesn't feel like reality is real anymore."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊啊啊！我知道啦！我只是感觉自己精神太累了，我都感受不到现实的真实感了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-8" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,8&#93;"><td id="西行寺幽幽子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">西行寺幽幽子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Weren't you going to ask Reimu and all of our Gensokyo friends about that?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"对于这种事你不是应该去问灵梦和你幻想乡的其他朋友吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-9" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,9&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah. We kind of got caught up in resolving the incident, though. Which I helped with, by the way! Everything will gradually go back to normal now."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"确实，不过我们当时在解决异变啦，我也帮了忙哦！现在世界应该正常了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-10" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,10&#93;"><td id="西行寺幽幽子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">西行寺幽幽子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You did well, Youmu. But I'd like to know, too, if the dream logic reached all the way over here. I'd be very unpleasantly surprised if it turned out those cherry trees were actually swizzle sticks all along."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"干得好啊妖梦，但咱也想知道梦逻辑是不是也入侵了白玉楼，如果咱的樱花树其实一直是木棍那我会很伤心的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-11" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,11&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"All right. I'm going to the Hakurei Shrine to see if Reimu and anyone else still there can help me sort things out."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"行吧，我现在去博丽神社看看我能帮上灵梦和其他人什么忙。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-12" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,12&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...That's all you remember? A huge garden of cherry trees around the manor?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"…你就记得大花园和宅子周围的樱花树了？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-13" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,13&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah. It's been a while since I've been to the Netherworld, but I don't think there were any glass trees or spatial distortions or anything."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是啊，我上次去冥界是很久之前了，但我不认为那里应该会有梦逻辑造成的棱镜花朵之类的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-14" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,14&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"That's exactly what it looks like now, too. Maybe the dream logic really did only affect Gensokyo."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"现在看确实是这样，或许梦逻辑真的只入侵了幻想乡啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-15" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,15&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"The Netherfolk did pretty well compared to us, huh?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"冥界肯定比我们这边好受多了吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-16" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,16&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Probably. I don't think I felt any different until I stepped into Gensokyo. "</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"差不多吧，我直到踏入幻想乡才发现了异常的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-17" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,17&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"That would make the most sense to me. Sure, the Miracle Mallet could grant someone the power to control THIS reality, but no source of magic I can conceive of would let someone control EVERY reality."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"这看起来是最具有说服力的提案了，万宝槌或许能给予某人控制我们现在这个幻想乡的现实的能力，但是应该不会有一种魔法能控制所有的境界的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-18" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,18&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Thank heavens for that. Imagine the Outside World recordin' all that with their satellites and cameras."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那真的感谢上帝了，想想如果这事发生在外界，那卫星和相机拍下来的东西可不好收拾。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-19" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,19&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Well, that's relieving. I wonder if it started influencing me as soon as I set foot here, though. That's what disturbs me the most about this. I'm not sure if how I'm acting right now is actually me, or, like...Aimi's preferred version of me."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，那我就放心了，我现在在想梦逻辑是不是在我一踏入幻想乡就开始影响我了，我也不确定现在的我是不是真的我，还是…爱美希望的我。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-20" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,20&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"For what it's worth, I haven't noticed you acting strangely at all."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"现在看来，我没有注意到你任何的异常啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-21" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,21&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You were just as eager as ever to resolve the incident, at any rate."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你不管在什么情况下都很积极的解决异变不是吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-22" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,22&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Although in my case, I think dream logic changing my personality is WHY I was so eager to resolve the incident. Funny how Aimi and Kiseki ended up orchestrating their own demise."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"不过对我来说就不一样了，我觉得梦逻辑改变了我的性格让我不再搁着异变不去退治了，所以爱美和剪世树这波是自己作死了。还挺好玩的。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-23" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,23&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Maybe we shouldn't worry about what's real and what's dream logic. We've settled the incident, after all. We'll know soon enough."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"可能我们现在没必要去想啥是真实的啥是梦逻辑了，不管咋说我们也解决了异变啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-24" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,24&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah, I probably should be thinking about it that way."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"没错的，我们应该用这个角度考虑。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-25" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,25&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"But you know...as weirded out as this whole existential crisis thing made me, I feel like I made a lot of great memories yesterday. I met Koishi. I helped Koishi reunite with this girl named Tetsuko who hadn't seen her in years. I helped make Kosuzu's first adventure a success. And of course, we resolved the incident."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"但…尽管这次是关幻想乡的生死存亡，我依旧觉得我很享受昨日这段时光。咱认识了恋恋，让她和铁子在数年不见后破镜重圆，我帮助了小铃完成了她的第一次冒险…当然最重要的，我们解决了异变。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-26" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,26&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Were you the one who decided we were all heroes of the poly...multi...something-verse?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你是那个和我们说我们都是多次…多元…多个平行啥啥宇宙的英雄来着的？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-27" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,27&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"It was Koishi, actually. But yes, that was another good memory."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那是恋恋啦，不过那确实也是一次美好的经历啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-28" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,28&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I know Tetsuko. I didn't know she knew Koishi, too. Maybe she really isn't as lonesome as she thinks she is."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我知道铁子，但是我不知道她居然认识恋恋啊，可能她并不像她自己想的那般孤独吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-29" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,29&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Aimi and Kiseki wanted to make people's dreams come true, and bringing people closer together was a big part of that, right? It feels like they really did accomplish that. I don't know if any of those memories would have been made yesterday if their dream logic hadn't been influencing us."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"爱美和剪世树希望人们的梦想成真，让人们互相理解拉近彼此的距离也是其中很重要的一环对吧？我能感觉到她们确确实实的做到了，如果梦逻辑没有影响我们的话，那昨天的种种美好回忆都不会发生了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-30" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,30&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Of course, they also accomplished really messing up reality, but is there a way we could...um...keep what we gained from this incident, while still fixing what was broken?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"不过她们搅乱现实境界依旧没得洗，有没有方法保留我们在这次异变中得到的东西，同时还能把幻想乡的现实修补好呢？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-31" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,31&#93;"><td id="茨木华扇" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">茨木华扇</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"We did talk to them about what they were going to do next. There's a few ways we came up with for them to help Gensokyo without almost destroying it. But once our free will is completely restored, what we take away from this experience is up to every individual person, and them alone."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我们和她们谈了接下来要做什么，对于她们来说，不毁掉幻想乡同时能帮它变得更好的方法当然是有的。但当我们的自由意志恢复后，我们从这次异变中能带回什么那就完全取决于个人自己了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-32" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,32&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm still figuring that out, but maybe there's things I can do to be a hero of Gensokyo...er, and the Netherworld too. Talk to more people, look for little ways to make their day, even if I don't expect anything in return. Watching all those things happen because of me yesterday just...felt good, you know? I want to do more of that, and I want it to truly be me doing it, not just a dream-logical version of me."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我大概还在思考这一点吧，但可能我依旧可以去做的事情，我依旧可以去做幻想乡…和冥界的英雄吧，和更多的人交谈，在微小细节上帮助他们，即便我不求回报。只是看着就好，因为我昨天的经历…真的让我感觉很好，你们大概明白吧？我想做更多这样的事情，而且我希望去做这些事情的是真正的我，而不是被梦逻辑影响的我啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-33" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,33&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...Well, that's what I think right now. We'll see what I think once I get my free will back. Heh."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...现在我就是这么想的，可能在我的自由意志回来后我会自由抉择吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-34" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,34&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm gonna take these neat glass flowers and plants and make super-weapons out of the dream logic magic in 'em. And I'll do that once my free will is back too."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我要把这些漂亮的棱镜植物做成梦幻超级武器，等着我的自由意志回来后就开工！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-35" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,35&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Marisa pulled a small glass rose out of some hidden pocket in her dress. Both the flower and the stem were semi-transparent, and small thorns decorated the stem.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魔理沙从她的裙子口袋里掏出了一枝小巧玲珑的棱镜玫瑰，花瓣和根茎都半透明的闪着光芒，根茎上布满了微小的尖刺。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-36" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,36&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Wow! I never examined one up close. These things are really well-made. I guess that's because they're crafted with magic instead of actual hands, huh? Though I guess there's something to be said for how the imperfections created by human hands are beautiful in their own right."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"哇！我之前从来没这么近距离观察这东西啊，做工真的很不错，我猜是因为她们是用魔法而不是双手制作它们的不是吗？不过我想人类双手造出来的错误也有它们独自的一种美吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-37" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,37&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I've got a couple more of this exact rose. Want this one to help ya remember?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我还有几个和这个一样的玫瑰哦。你想来一枝来纪念一下这次事件吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-38" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,38&#93;"><td id="魂魄妖梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">魂魄妖梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Really? You're gonna part with that rare magical object, just like that? I mean, sure!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"诶？你真的要把这么稀有的魔法物件送给我吗？…我的意思是，当然要！不胜感激！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-39" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,39&#93;"><td id="博丽灵梦" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">博丽灵梦</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Better take it before Marisa loses her dream logic niceness."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"在魔理沙失掉她的梦逻辑善意之前抓紧收了吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-40" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,40&#93;"><td id="雾雨魔理沙" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">雾雨魔理沙</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Hey! I'd do this normally too! I mean, maybe I would. I dunno."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"喂！我平时也有这么做吧！我想是的…呃…大概会吧，我也不知道了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-41" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,41&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">After a few more formalities, Youmu began her trip back to the Netherworld, but she couldn't help but linger, staring wistfully at the surreal environmental features that still dotted the landscape. Aimi and Kiseki had put so much effort into making the trees, flowers and sky so colorful and precisely-crafted...</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">在大家又聊了几句后，妖梦启程准备回冥界，但她怀念的目光忍不住定格在梦逻辑造成的种种上，爱美和剪世树真的花了好大功夫制作这些花草树木和广阔天地啊。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-42" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,42&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Youmu snapped out of her trance. There was no point in being sad. Those beautiful decorations had to go away no matter what; the only thing anyone could do was look ahead to the future. Feeling the glass flower in her pocket again, Youmu turned toward the Netherworld and sped home without looking back.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">妖梦从这惆怅里抽身而出，悲伤没有任何意义，这些美丽的装饰不管怎样总会消失的，我们只能向前眺望未来，感受到了口袋中棱镜玫瑰的共鸣，她不回头的奔向了远方的冥界入口。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-43" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,43&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Mm-hm. I thought that might be the reason you came to live in the middle of nowhere. I understand. Everyone was afraid of my sister and I because we're satoris and we could read people's minds."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"嗯，我想这就是你居住在这森林里的原因了吧。我很懂这种感觉哦，所有人都害怕我姐姐，因为我们是可以阅读人心的觉妖怪。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-44" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,44&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"So I thought, if I closed my Third Eye, surely I wouldn't be able to read minds anymore, right? Well, I was right, but it seems that in the process I sealed away my own mind. All this stuff I'm saying and doing right now? That's just my subconscious."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"所以我就想如果我闭上我的第三只眼睛，那我就肯定读不了心了吧？确实是这样的，但问题是在这个过程中我也封闭了自己的念想，我现在说的做的都只是潜意识罢了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-45" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,45&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"And unless I get their attention and they can focus on me, other people can't perceive me consciously either. And they'll forget about me as soon as I leave, except if they already knew about me. Then it's easier to remember. What a life, huh?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"还有除非我得到人们的注意，他们也没法清晰地意识到我的存在，并且我一旦离开他们就会淡忘我，除非他们之前就记得我，多么美好的日子啊不是吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-46" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,46&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"You know, I had a feeling that's what your Third Eye was for. But if that's true, how was I able to remember you?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你知道吗，我其实隐隐猜到了你第三只眼睛的事情，但如果你说的是真的的话，我怎么能记得你呢？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-47" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,47&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Sometimes children are able to see me because their minds are still growing. But once they grow up they forget about me just like everyone else. You must be something special if you were able to remember me after all these years, Tetsuko!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"有些时候，孩子们能看见我，因为他们的思想意识还在不断生长成熟，但是一旦他们长大了就会像其他人一样忘了我，能记得我这么长时间的铁子你，一定很特别吧！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-48" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,48&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Well, maybe it's just because I liked your company better than that of anyone in the village."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，可能是因为比起村子里的所有人，我更喜欢你的陪伴。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-49" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,49&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Tetsuko's gaze seemed to wander into space. Koishi worried for a moment that she'd become unperceivable again, but Tetsuko restored eye contact with her after a few seconds.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铁子的目光似乎神游去了宇宙，恋恋在那瞬间很害怕她又看不见自己了，不过几秒后她们的目光又对上了。</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-50" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,50&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Koishi, where did you meet that Youmu girl?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"恋恋啊，你在哪里认识的那女孩妖梦啊？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-51" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,51&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Oh, we just happened to run into each other while we were trying to figure out the dream logic. Everyone's enhanced self-awareness and empathy probably made more people able to notice me."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"啊，我们只是碰巧在分析梦逻辑的时候撞上了，梦逻辑给大家增强的自我意识和同情心大概让大家更能看见我吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-52" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,52&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I see. And if you're familiar with danmaku, that must mean you've dueled with other people in the past?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我明白了，还有你对弹幕这么熟悉，肯定是因为你在之前和其他人打过架吧？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-53" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,53&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yep! Oh wait, you wouldn't know about that, would you."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那是当然！我把人类村宗教战争的所有遇见的人都一顿痛扁了！哦对了，你肯定不知道这回事吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-54" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,54&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I don't. But it sounds like at least a few people have come to know you, despite your...circumstance, right?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那是当然，不过听起来哪怕你干了这么多丰功伟绩，认识你的人还是很少啊。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-55" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,55&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yeah. It's something I hadn't gotten a taste of since sealing away my Third Eye."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"确实，做一个无意识的漫游者是很有意思，但是当我第一次和灵梦魔理沙战斗后，幻想乡更多的人知道了我的存在，这…确实很有趣的你知道吗？这种感觉在我封印了自己的第三只眼后就没再尝过了。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-56" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,56&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"One of the other incident-resolvers...Sanae, that was her name. Anyway, though, uh...do you want to visit the shrine?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"好极了！那里的神明很是强大哦！信仰她们准没错的，她们还给我姐姐的宠物加装了核大炮！如果用那种东西点亮幻想乡大概会有多好玩呢？！当然这是个烂主意别想了…不过说回来，你想去吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-58" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,58&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm...not sure. Yesterday, I got a taste of something like that too, when dream logic kept pushing me toward other people. I didn't want to be around them, but somehow...at the same time, I did want to be around them. And they didn't seem repulsed by the fact that I could read their emotions. So I can't help but wonder if trying to interact with people again would be worth it."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我…我不确定啊，昨天其实我也有一些被梦逻辑驱使去与其他人拉近距离的倾向。我不想呆在他们身边，但我又有点…想在他们身边。然后他们也没有因为我可以阅读他们的情绪而排斥我，所以我不自觉的思考值不值得在再别人交往。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-59" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,59&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I say go for it! What do you have to lose?!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我说干就完了！你也没有什么可失去的不是吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-60" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,60&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"They might be uncomfortable once I've been around them reading their emotions for too long."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"如果我读取他们的情绪太长时间了他们可能会讨厌我吧。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-61" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,61&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Can you know whether that'll happen until you try?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你在尝试之前就知道会发生什么吗？"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-62" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,62&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Well, no."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"那倒不能。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-63" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,63&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"And you said you were perfectly content living away from everyone else in this forest. You don't NEED relationships. You're just going to try them out. So if it doesn't work out, you can just go back to exactly how you are now and you'll be perfectly content. Right?"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"你还说你在这个与世无争的森林里过的完美的日子呢。你不一定需要人际关系，但你要去试试，如果不行的话你再回这里完美的种你的田。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-64" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,64&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Yes."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"是的，你说的没错。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-65" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,65&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"So it seems to me like you have nothing to lose and some cool stuff to gain!"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"看！你什么都没失去，而且还可能得到一些好东西呢！"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-66" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,66&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"All right. I'll try it. When I feel ready, that is."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"好的，我会去尝试的，当我准备好的时候。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-67" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,67&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"Of course. No rush."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"当然当然，无需着急。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-68" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,68&#93;"><td id="旁白" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">旁白</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Tetsuko stretched her arms and then retreated to the door behind her. It led into a small home built into a hillside cave, with a single artificial wall made of tied-together branches.</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">铁子伸展了一下她的手臂退回到了门后，门后是她依山而的小房子，外层是树枝绑起来的围墙</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-69" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,69&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"I'm exhausted, so I think I'll go inside now, but thank you for coming by, Koishi."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"我太累了恋恋，咱要回屋休息了，不过感谢你来拜访我。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-70" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,70&#93;"><td id="古明地恋" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">古明地恋</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"It was a pleasure to see you again, Tetsuko. I look forward to hearing legends of your exploits as a nuclear-fire-cannon-wielding superhero of Gensokyo."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"能再见到你我也很高兴铁子，我希望之后也能听到你那核大炮幻想乡超级英雄的故事啊"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-content" id="Ending_No._05-71" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,71&#93;"><td id="夜花铁子" class="tt-char" lang="zh"><div class="poem">夜花铁子</div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">"...Heh."</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">"...好好。"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._05-72" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,72&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Principle of Non-Contradiction Team's Ending: "Something to Take With Us"</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">无矛盾律组结局: "满载而归的宝物"</div></td></tr><tr class="tt-header" id="Ending_No._05-73" data-pos="&#91;&quot;Ending No. 05&quot;,73&#93;"><td id="" class="tt-h" lang="zh"><div class="poem"></div></td><td class="tt-ja" lang="ja"><div class="poem">Congratulations on a 1-credit clear!</div></td><td class="tt-zh" lang="zh"><div class="poem">恭喜 1-credit 通关！</div></td></tr></tbody></table>

ENDING No.5 插图





[^cite_note-1]: 根据音乐评论，T.N.G.的意思是“中立的少女”（The Netural Girl）。
